const ALL_PHONES=D.telefon||[];const ALL_TABLET=D.tablet||[];const ALL_NOTEBOOK=D.notebook||[];const ALL_AKSESUAR=D.aksesuar||[];const ALL_VINN=D.vinn||[];
const fmt=n=>n?.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g,".")||"0";
const is5G=m=>/S25|A17.5G|A26.5G|Y29S|iPhone.1[5-9]|iPhone.Air/i.test(m);

// TAKSIT KURALLARI:
// Aksesuar: herkese 36 aya kadar tüm taksitler
// Telefon/Tablet/Notebook ≤30K: 3,6,9,12 ay (herkese)
// Telefon/Tablet/Notebook >30K: sadece 3 ay (normal), 12+ kurumsal
const getVTaksit=(p,isAksesuar)=>{
  const r=[];
  if(p.t3>0)r.push({vade:3,aylik:p.t3,toplam:p.t3t});
  if(p.t6>0)r.push({vade:6,aylik:p.t6,toplam:p.t6t});
  if(p.t9>0)r.push({vade:9,aylik:p.t9,toplam:p.t9t});
  if(p.t12>0)r.push({vade:12,aylik:p.t12,toplam:p.t12t});
  if(p.t24>0)r.push({vade:24,aylik:p.t24,toplam:p.t24t});
  if(p.t36>0)r.push({vade:36,aylik:p.t36,toplam:p.t36t});
  if(isAksesuar) return r; // aksesuar: herkese hepsi
  if((p.p||0)>30000) return r.filter(t=>t.vade<=3); // >30K: sadece 3 ay
  return r.filter(t=>t.vade<=12); // ≤30K: 3,6,9,12 ay
};

const allDevices={phone:ALL_PHONES.map(p=>({marka:p.m,model:p.n,pesin:p.p,pesinIndirimli:p.pi,...p})),tablet:ALL_TABLET.map(p=>({marka:p.m,model:p.n,pesin:p.p,pesinIndirimli:p.pi,...p})),notebook:ALL_NOTEBOOK.map(p=>({marka:p.m,model:p.n,pesin:p.p,pesinIndirimli:p.pi,...p})),aksesuar:ALL_AKSESUAR.map(p=>({marka:p.m,model:p.n,pesin:p.p,pesinIndirimli:p.pi,...p}))};

/* ═══ SPLASH ═══ */
function Splash({onClick}){
  return(<div style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,zIndex:9999,background:"#0d1b3e",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",animation:"splashBg 4s ease-in-out forwards",overflow:"hidden"}} onClick={onClick}>
    <img src={INTRO_IMG} alt="Kampanya" style={{maxWidth:"100%",maxHeight:"100vh",objectFit:"contain",animation:"splashZoom 4s ease-in-out forwards"}}/>
    <div style={{position:"absolute",bottom:40,left:0,right:0,textAlign:"center",animation:"splashTxt 4s ease-in-out forwards"}}>
      <div style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.92)",backdropFilter:"blur(10px)",display:"inline-flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8,padding:"10px 24px",borderRadius:14}}>
        <img src={LOGO_ICON} alt="" style={{height:24}}/>
        <div style={{textAlign:"left"}}><div style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:800,letterSpacing:1}}>ELFİN İLETİŞİM</div><div style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>Turkcell Yetkili Bayi • Konya</div></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style={{position:"absolute",bottom:12,width:"100%",textAlign:"center",animation:"splashTxt 4s ease-in-out forwards"}}><span style={{fontSize:10,color:"rgba(255,255,255,.4)"}}>Atlamak için dokunun</span></div>
  </div>);
}

/* ═══ MOBILE MENU ═══ */
function MobileMenu({page,setPage,user,onAuth,onAdmin,isAdmin}){
  return(<div style={{background:"#fff",borderBottom:"1px solid var(--brd)",padding:"8px 20px",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:2}}>
    {[{k:"home",l:"🏠 Ana Sayfa"},{k:"phone",l:"📱 Telefon"},{k:"tablet",l:"📋 Tablet"},{k:"notebook",l:"💻 Notebook"},{k:"aksesuar",l:"🎧 Aksesuar"},{k:"tariff",l:"📡 Tarifeler"},{k:"contact",l:"📍 İletişim"}].map(n=>(
      <button key={n.k} onClick={()=>setPage(n.k)} style={{background:page===n.k?"var(--blt)":"transparent",border:"none",color:page===n.k?"var(--acc)":"var(--txt2)",padding:"10px 14px",borderRadius:8,fontSize:13,fontWeight:600,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",textAlign:"left"}}>{n.l}</button>
    ))}
    <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,marginTop:4}}>
      {isAdmin&&<button onClick={onAdmin} style={{flex:1,background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",color:"var(--txt2)",padding:"10px",borderRadius:8,fontSize:12,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>⚙️ Yönetim</button>}
      <button onClick={onAuth} style={{flex:1,background:"var(--acc)",border:"none",color:"#fff",padding:"10px",borderRadius:8,fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{user||"Giriş Yap"}</button>
    </div>
  </div>);
}

/* ═══ WAVE TEXT BANNER ═══ */
function WaveText({text, baseDelay=0}) {
  return (<span>{text.split("").map((ch,i) => (
    <span key={i} style={{display:"inline-block",animation:`waveChar 2.5s ease-in-out ${baseDelay + i * 0.06}s infinite`,whiteSpace:ch===" "?"pre":"normal"}}>{ch}</span>
  ))}</span>);
}

function WaveBanner() {
  return (
    <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#253B80,#1a2d62)",borderRadius:16,padding:"20px 20px 16px",maxWidth:540,margin:"0 auto 12px",textAlign:"center",overflow:"hidden",position:"relative"}}>
      <div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:"100%",background:"linear-gradient(90deg,transparent,rgba(255,255,255,.03),transparent)",backgroundSize:"200% 100%",animation:"shimmerBg 3s linear infinite"}} />
      <div style={{position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--tc)",fontWeight:800,letterSpacing:2}}>2026 SONUNA KADAR</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:900,lineHeight:1.3,marginTop:6}}>
          <WaveText text="ANINDA " baseDelay={0} />
          <span style={{display:"inline"}}>{" "}</span>
          <span style={{color:"var(--tc)",fontSize:24}}><WaveText text="200 TL" baseDelay={0.5} /></span>
        </div>
        <div style={{fontSize:17,fontWeight:900,marginTop:2}}>
          <WaveText text="ALIŞVERİŞ ÇEKİ" baseDelay={0.8} />
        </div>
        <div style={{fontSize:11,color:"rgba(255,255,255,.6)",marginTop:8}}>Faturalıya Geçiş veya Yeni Hat Alımına</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--tc)",marginTop:6,fontWeight:700}}>+ iPHONE 15 ÇEKİLİŞİ — Her faturalı işleme çekiliş hakkı!</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ═══ COUNTDOWN BANNER ═══ */
function CountdownBanner() {
  const[time,setTime]=useState({d:0,h:0,m:0,s:0});
  useEffect(()=>{
    const target=new Date("2026-04-01T00:00:00+03:00").getTime();
    const calc=()=>{
      const now=Date.now();const diff=Math.max(0,target-now);
      setTime({d:Math.floor(diff/86400000),h:Math.floor((diff%86400000)/3600000),m:Math.floor((diff%3600000)/60000),s:Math.floor((diff%60000)/1000)});
    };
    calc();const t=setInterval(calc,1000);return()=>clearInterval(t);
  },[]);
  const isLive=time.d===0&&time.h===0&&time.m===0&&time.s===0;
  return(
    <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#0d7c3d,#15a050)",borderRadius:14,padding:"16px 20px",maxWidth:540,margin:"0 auto 24px",overflow:"hidden",position:"relative"}}>
      <div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:"100%",background:"linear-gradient(90deg,transparent,rgba(255,255,255,.04),transparent)",backgroundSize:"200% 100%",animation:"shimmerBg 4s linear infinite"}} />
      <div style={{position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
        <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",gap:10,marginBottom:10}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:24}}>⚡</span>
          <div style={{textAlign:"left"}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:900,color:"#fff"}}>{isLive?"5G YAYINDA!":"1 NİSAN'DA 5G BAŞLIYOR!"}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"rgba(255,255,255,.75)"}}>Galaxy S25 • iPhone 15 • Vivo Y29S • Samsung A17 5G</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {!isLive&&(
          <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,justifyContent:"center"}}>
            {[{v:time.d,l:"GÜN"},{v:time.h,l:"SAAT"},{v:time.m,l:"DAKİKA"},{v:time.s,l:"SANİYE"}].map((u,i)=>(
              <div key={i} style={{background:"rgba(0,0,0,.25)",borderRadius:10,padding:"8px 4px",minWidth:52,textAlign:"center",backdropFilter:"blur(4px)"}}>
                <div style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:900,color:"#fff",lineHeight:1,animation:u.l==="SANİYE"?"countPulse 1s infinite":"none"}}>{String(u.v).padStart(2,"0")}</div>
                <div style={{fontSize:7,color:"rgba(255,255,255,.6)",fontWeight:700,letterSpacing:1,marginTop:3}}>{u.l}</div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        {isLive&&<div style={{textAlign:"center",fontSize:18,fontWeight:900,color:"#fff",animation:"countPulse 1.5s infinite"}}>🎉 5G ARTIK AKTİF!</div>}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ═══ HOME ═══ */
function Home({onNav}){

          <div key={i} className="ac" onClick={()=>onNav(s.k)} style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:12,padding:16,textAlign:"center",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",animationDelay:`${i*.07}s`,animationFillMode:"both",cursor:"pointer",transition:"all .2s",boxShadow:"var(--sh)"}}
            onMouseEnter={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="translateY(-2px)";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="0 6px 18px rgba(37,59,128,.1)"}}
            onMouseLeave={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="var(--sh)"}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:900,color:s.c}}>{s.n}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",marginTop:2}}>{s.l}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:8,color:s.c,marginTop:4,fontWeight:600}}>{"Görüntüle →"}</div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ═══ DEVICE PAGE ═══ */
function DevicePage({data,title,sub,isAksesuar,onSelectedChange}){
  const[search,setSearch]=useState("");const[brand,setBrand]=useState("all");const[maxPrice,setMaxPrice]=useState(0);const[sortBy,setSortBy]=useState("price_asc");const[selected,setSelected]=useState(null);
  const brands=useMemo(()=>["all",...[...new Set(data.map(d=>d.marka))].sort()],[data]);
  const priceMax=useMemo(()=>Math.max(...data.map(d=>d.pesin)),[data]);
  const filtered=useMemo(()=>{
    let f=data.filter(d=>{if(brand!=="all"&&d.marka!==brand)return false;if(maxPrice>0&&d.pesin>maxPrice)return false;if(search){const q=search.toLowerCase();const full=(d.marka+" "+d.model).toLowerCase();return q.split(/\s+/).some(w=>w.length>0&&full.includes(w))}return true});
    if(sortBy==="price_asc")f.sort((a,b)=>a.pesin-b.pesin);else if(sortBy==="price_desc")f.sort((a,b)=>b.pesin-a.pesin);else f.sort((a,b)=>a.model.localeCompare(b.model));
    return f;
  },[data,brand,maxPrice,search,sortBy]);

  // Register selected reset with parent for back button
  useEffect(()=>{
    if(onSelectedChange){
      onSelectedChange(selected?()=>setSelected(null):null);
    }
  },[selected,onSelectedChange]);

  return(
    <div className="au" style={{paddingTop:28}}>
      <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:18}}><h2 style={{fontFamily:"'Playfair Display',serif",fontSize:"clamp(20px,3.5vw,30px)",fontWeight:800,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:4}}>{title}</h2><p style={{fontSize:12,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>{sub}</p></div>
      <div style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:12,padding:14,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",marginBottom:16,boxShadow:"var(--sh)"}}>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,marginBottom:10,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
          <input value={search} onChange={e=>setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="🔍 Model ara..." style={{flex:"1 1 160px",padding:"9px 12px",background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,color:"var(--txt)",fontSize:13,fontFamily:"inherit",outline:"none"}}/>
          <select value={sortBy} onChange={e=>setSortBy(e.target.value)} style={{padding:"9px 12px",background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,color:"var(--txt)",fontSize:11,fontFamily:"inherit"}}><option value="price_asc">{"Fiyat ↑"}</option><option value="price_desc">{"Fiyat ↓"}</option><option value="name">A-Z</option></select>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:4,flexWrap:"wrap",marginBottom:10}}>
          {brands.slice(0,18).map(b=>(<button key={b} onClick={()=>setBrand(b)} style={{background:brand===b?"var(--acc)":"var(--bg2)",color:brand===b?"#fff":"var(--txt2)",border:"1px solid "+(brand===b?"var(--acc)":"var(--brd)"),borderRadius:6,padding:"4px 9px",fontSize:10,fontWeight:600,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{b==="all"?"Tümü":b}</button>))}
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8}}><span style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>Maks:</span><input type="range" min={0} max={priceMax} step={1000} value={maxPrice} onChange={e=>setMaxPrice(Number(e.target.value))} style={{flex:1}}/><span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)",minWidth:70,textAlign:"right"}}>{maxPrice===0?"Tümü":`₺${fmt(maxPrice)}`}</span></div>
      </div>
      <div style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--txt3)",marginBottom:8}}>{filtered.length} ürün</div>
      {selected?(<div>
        <div style={{marginBottom:14}}>
          <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:6}}><span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>Ürünler</span><button onClick={()=>setSelected(null)} style={{background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",color:"var(--txt3)",padding:"3px 9px",borderRadius:5,fontSize:10,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>✕ Kapat</button></div>
          <div style={{display:"flex",gap:5,overflowX:"auto",paddingBottom:4,WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
            {filtered.map(d=>(<button key={d.id} onClick={()=>setSelected(d)} style={{flex:"0 0 auto",background:selected.id===d.id?"var(--blt)":"#fff",border:selected.id===d.id?"2px solid var(--acc)":"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 10px",cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",color:"var(--txt)",minWidth:110,textAlign:"left"}}>
              <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:4}}><span style={{fontSize:8,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)"}}>{d.marka}</span>{is5G(d.model)&&<Badge5G/>}</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:600,marginTop:1}}>{d.model}</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--tcD)",marginTop:2}}>₺{fmt(d.pesin)}</div>
            </button>))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <DeviceDetail d={selected} isAksesuar={isAksesuar}/>
      </div>):(<div className="grid-cards" style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(250px,1fr))",gap:12}}>
        {filtered.map((d,i)=><DeviceCard key={d.id} d={d} i={i} onClick={()=>setSelected(d)} isAksesuar={isAksesuar}/>)}
      </div>)}
      {filtered.length===0&&<Empty/>}
    </div>
  );
}

function Badge5G(){return <span style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#0d7c3d,#15a050)",color:"#fff",fontSize:8,fontWeight:800,padding:"1px 5px",borderRadius:4,letterSpacing:.3}}>5G</span>}

function DeviceCard({d,i,onClick,isAksesuar}){
  const vt=getVTaksit(d,isAksesuar);const best=vt.length?vt.reduce((a,b)=>a.vade>b.vade?a:b):null;const f5=is5G(d.model);const over30=d.pesin>30000&&!isAksesuar;
  return(
    <div className="ac" onClick={onClick} style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:12,padding:16,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",cursor:"pointer",animationDelay:`${Math.min(i*.03,.35)}s`,animationFillMode:"both",transition:"all .2s",boxShadow:"var(--sh)",position:"relative",overflow:"hidden"}}
      onMouseEnter={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="translateY(-2px)";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="0 6px 20px rgba(37,59,128,.1)"}}
      onMouseLeave={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="var(--sh)"}}>
      {f5&&<div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:3,background:"linear-gradient(90deg,#0d7c3d,#15a050)"}}/>}
      {!f5&&<div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:2,background:"linear-gradient(90deg,var(--acc),var(--tc))"}}/>}
      <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:5,marginBottom:3}}>
        <span style={{fontSize:9,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:700,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:1}}>{d.marka}</span>
        {f5&&<Badge5G/>}
        {over30&&<span style={{fontSize:7,color:"var(--acc)",background:"var(--blt)",padding:"1px 5px",borderRadius:3,fontWeight:600}}>Kurumsal Taksit</span>}
      </div>
      <h3 style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--txt)",marginBottom:8,lineHeight:1.2}}>{d.model}</h3>
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:5,flexWrap:"wrap",marginBottom:6}}>
        <Chip label="Peşin" value={`₺${fmt(d.pesinIndirimli||d.pesin)}`} accent/>
        {best&&<Chip label={`${best.vade} Ay`} value={`₺${fmt(Math.round(best.aylik))}/ay`}/>}
      </div>
      {vt.length>0&&<div style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{vt.map(t=>`${t.vade}ay`).join(" • ")} taksit{over30?" (Kurumsal)":""}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}
function Chip({label,value,accent}){return(<div style={{background:accent?"rgba(255,199,44,.1)":"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:6,padding:"4px 7px",textAlign:"center"}}><div style={{fontSize:7,color:"var(--txt3)",fontWeight:600,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:.3}}>{label}</div><div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:800,color:accent?"var(--tcD)":"var(--txt)"}}>{value}</div></div>)}

function DeviceDetail({d,isAksesuar}){
  const vt=getVTaksit(d,isAksesuar);const f5=is5G(d.model);const over30=d.pesin>30000&&!isAksesuar;
  return(
    <div className="au" style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:16,padding:22,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",boxShadow:"0 4px 20px rgba(37,59,128,.07)",animation:"glow 3s ease-in-out infinite"}}>
      <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"flex-start",flexWrap:"wrap",gap:10,marginBottom:16}}>
        <div>
          <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:6,marginBottom:2}}>
            <span style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:700,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:2}}>{d.marka}</span>
            {f5&&<Badge5G/>}
          </div>
          <h2 style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--txt)"}}>{d.model}</h2>
        </div>
        <div style={{textAlign:"right"}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt3)",fontWeight:600,textTransform:"uppercase"}}>Peşin</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:26,fontWeight:900,color:"var(--acc)"}}>₺{fmt(d.pesinIndirimli||d.pesin)}</div>
          {d.pesinIndirimli&&d.pesinIndirimli<d.pesin&&<div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",textDecoration:"line-through"}}>₺{fmt(d.pesin)}</div>}
        </div>
      </div>
      {over30&&<div style={{background:"var(--blt)",borderRadius:8,padding:"8px 12px",marginBottom:14,fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:600}}>ℹ️ 30.000 TL üzeri cihazlarda normal müşteriye sadece 3 ay taksit. İşletme sahibi (vergi levhası) müşterilere 12 ay ve üzeri taksit imkanı mevcuttur — detay için mağazamızı arayın: 0532 682 22 77</div>}
      {vt.length>0&&(
        <div className="detail-grid" style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:`repeat(${Math.min(vt.length,4)},1fr)`,gap:8,marginBottom:16}}>
          {vt.map(t=>{const fark=t.toplam-d.pesin;return(
            <div key={t.vade} style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:10,padding:12,textAlign:"center",border:"1px solid var(--brd)"}}>
              <div style={{fontSize:7,color:"var(--txt3)",fontWeight:600,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:1,marginBottom:3}}>{t.vade} Taksit</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:16,fontWeight:900,color:"var(--acc)"}}>₺{fmt(Math.round(t.aylik))}</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>/ ay</div>
              <div style={{marginTop:4,height:3,background:"var(--brd)",borderRadius:2,overflow:"hidden"}}><div style={{width:`${Math.min((d.pesin/t.toplam)*100,100)}%`,height:"100%",background:"linear-gradient(90deg,var(--acc),var(--tc))",borderRadius:2}}/></div>
              <div style={{fontSize:7,color:"var(--txt3)",marginTop:2}}>Toplam: ₺{fmt(t.toplam)}</div>
              {fark>0&&<div style={{fontSize:7,color:"#D4548A",marginTop:1}}>+₺{fmt(fark)} fark</div>}
            </div>
          );})}
        </div>
      )}
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
        <a href={waLink(d.marka+" "+d.model,d.pesinIndirimli||d.pesin)} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" style={{flex:1,minWidth:140,background:"#25D366",border:"none",borderRadius:10,padding:12,color:"#fff",fontWeight:800,fontSize:13,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",textDecoration:"none",textAlign:"center",boxShadow:"0 4px 12px rgba(37,166,104,.25)"}}>💬 WhatsApp ile Bilgi Al</a>
        <a href="tel:05326822277" style={{background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:10,padding:"12px 16px",color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:600,fontSize:12,textDecoration:"none",display:"flex",alignItems:"center"}}>📞 Ara</a>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ═══ TARIFF PAGE ═══ */
function TariffPage({tariffs}){
  const[tip,setTip]=useState("faturali");const[gbMin,setGbMin]=useState(0);const[dkMin,setDkMin]=useState(0);const[selectedCat,setSelectedCat]=useState(null);const[selectedTariff,setSelectedTariff]=useState(null);const[tSearch,setTSearch]=useState("");
  const cats=tariffs.filter(c=>c.tip===tip);
  const allT=cats.flatMap(c=>c.tarifeler.map(t=>({...t,kategori:c.ad,sart:c.sart,aciklama:c.aciklama,sure:c.sure,ikon:c.ikon,renk:c.renk,tip:c.tip})));
  const filtered=allT.filter(t=>{if(gbMin>0&&t.gb<gbMin)return false;if(dkMin>0&&t.dk<dkMin)return false;if(selectedCat&&t.kategori!==selectedCat)return false;if(tSearch){const q=tSearch.toLowerCase();return(t.ad+" "+t.kategori+" "+t.icerik+" "+t.gb+"gb").toLowerCase().includes(q)}return true}).sort((a,b)=>a.fiyat-b.fiyat);
  return(
    <div className="au" style={{paddingTop:28}}>
      <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:18}}><h2 style={{fontFamily:"'Playfair Display',serif",fontSize:"clamp(20px,3.5vw,30px)",fontWeight:800,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:4}}>Turkcell Tarifeleri</h2><p style={{fontSize:12,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>20 kategori, 88 tarife</p></div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,justifyContent:"center",marginBottom:16,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
        {[{k:"faturali",l:"📄 Faturalı"},{k:"onodemeli",l:"💳 Ön Ödemeli"}].map(b=>(<button key={b.k} onClick={()=>{setTip(b.k);setSelectedCat(null);setSelectedTariff(null);setTSearch("")}} style={{background:tip===b.k?"var(--acc)":"#fff",color:tip===b.k?"#fff":"var(--txt2)",border:tip===b.k?"none":"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:12,padding:"10px 24px",fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",boxShadow:tip===b.k?"0 4px 10px rgba(37,59,128,.18)":"var(--sh)"}}>{b.l}</button>))}
      </div>
      <div style={{maxWidth:400,margin:"0 auto 16px"}}>
        <input value={tSearch} onChange={e=>setTSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="🔍 Tarife ara... (örn: 30 GB, genç, emekli)" style={{width:"100%",padding:"10px 14px",background:"#fff",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:10,color:"var(--txt)",fontSize:13,fontFamily:"inherit",outline:"none",boxShadow:"var(--sh)"}}/>
      </div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:6,flexWrap:"wrap",justifyContent:"center",marginBottom:16}}>
        <button onClick={()=>{setSelectedCat(null);setSelectedTariff(null)}} style={{background:!selectedCat?"var(--tc)":"#fff",color:!selectedCat?"var(--txt)":"var(--txt2)",border:"1px solid "+(!selectedCat?"var(--tc)":"var(--brd)"),borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 14px",fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>Tümü</button>
        {cats.map(c=>(<button key={c.ad} onClick={()=>{setSelectedCat(c.ad);setSelectedTariff(null)}} style={{background:selectedCat===c.ad?"var(--blt)":"#fff",color:selectedCat===c.ad?"var(--acc)":"var(--txt2)",border:`1px solid ${selectedCat===c.ad?"var(--acc)":"var(--brd)"}`,borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 14px",fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{c.ikon} {c.ad}</button>))}
      </div>
      {tip==="faturali"&&(<div style={{display:"flex",gap:6,overflowX:"auto",marginBottom:14,paddingBottom:4,WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
        {Object.entries(SART_INFO).map(([k,s])=>(<div key={k} style={{flex:"0 0 auto",background:"#fff",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 12px",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:6,minWidth:160,boxShadow:"var(--sh)"}}><span style={{fontSize:16}}>{s.i}</span><div><div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:700,color:s.r}}>{s.b}</div><div style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt3)",lineHeight:1.2}}>{s.a}</div></div></div>))}
      </div>)}
      {tip==="onodemeli"&&<div style={{background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,padding:"8px 14px",marginBottom:14,fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:600}}>Ön ödemeli tarifelerde şart aranmaz.</div>}
      <div style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:12,padding:14,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",marginBottom:16,boxShadow:"var(--sh)"}}>
        <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(200px,1fr))",gap:14}}>
          <RSlider label="🌐 Min. İnternet" value={gbMin} max={100} step={5} unit="GB" color="var(--acc)" onChange={setGbMin}/>
          <RSlider label="📞 Min. Dakika" value={dkMin} max={3000} step={500} unit="dk" color="#3A5BC7" onChange={setDkMin}/>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--txt3)",marginBottom:8}}>{filtered.length} tarife</div>
      {selectedTariff?(<div>
        <div style={{marginBottom:14}}>
          <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:6}}><span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>Tarifeler</span><button onClick={()=>setSelectedTariff(null)} style={{background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",color:"var(--txt3)",padding:"3px 9px",borderRadius:5,fontSize:10,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>✕ Kapat</button></div>
          <div style={{display:"flex",gap:5,overflowX:"auto",paddingBottom:4,WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
            {filtered.map((t,i)=>(<button key={i} onClick={()=>setSelectedTariff(t)} style={{flex:"0 0 auto",background:selectedTariff.ad===t.ad&&selectedTariff.fiyat===t.fiyat?"var(--blt)":"#fff",border:selectedTariff.ad===t.ad&&selectedTariff.fiyat===t.fiyat?"2px solid var(--acc)":"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 10px",cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",color:"var(--txt)",minWidth:100,textAlign:"left"}}><div style={{fontSize:13}}>{t.ikon}</div><div style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)"}}>{t.ad}</div><div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:800}}>₺{t.fiyat}</div></button>))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <TariffDetail t={selectedTariff}/>
      </div>):(<div className="grid-cards" style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(270px,1fr))",gap:12}}>
        {filtered.map((t,i)=><TariffCard key={i} t={t} i={i} onClick={()=>setSelectedTariff(t)}/>)}
      </div>)}
      {filtered.length===0&&<Empty/>}
    </div>
  );
}
function RSlider({label,value,max,step,unit,color,onChange}){return(<div><div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:5}}><span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:600,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>{label}</span><span style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color,minWidth:60,textAlign:"right"}}>{value===0?"Tümü":`${value}+ ${unit}`}</span></div><input type="range" min={0} max={max} step={step} value={value} onChange={e=>onChange(Number(e.target.value))}/></div>)}
function TariffCard({t,i,onClick}){
  const hasSart=t.sart&&SART_INFO[t.sart];
  return(<div className="ac" onClick={onClick} style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:12,padding:16,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",cursor:"pointer",animationDelay:`${Math.min(i*.05,.35)}s`,animationFillMode:"both",transition:"all .2s",boxShadow:"var(--sh)",position:"relative",overflow:"hidden"}}
    onMouseEnter={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="translateY(-2px)";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="0 6px 18px rgba(37,59,128,.1)"}} onMouseLeave={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.transform="";e.currentTarget.style.boxShadow="var(--sh)"}}>
    <div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:3,background:"linear-gradient(90deg,var(--acc),var(--tc))"}}/>
    {hasSart&&<div style={{position:"absolute",top:8,right:8,background:"var(--blt)",color:"var(--acc)",fontSize:7,fontWeight:700,padding:"2px 6px",borderRadius:4}}>{SART_INFO[t.sart].b}</div>}
    <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8,marginBottom:12}}><div style={{width:38,height:38,borderRadius:10,background:"var(--blt)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:18}}>{t.ikon}</div><div><div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--txt)"}}>{t.ad}</div><div style={{fontSize:9,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{t.sure} • {t.kategori}</div></div></div>
    <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr",gap:5,marginBottom:10}}>
      <TStat l="İnternet" v={`${t.gb}GB`} c="var(--acc)"/><TStat l="Dakika" v={`${t.dk}`} c="#3A5BC7"/><TStat l="SMS" v={`${t.sms}`} c="#D4548A"/>
    </div>
    <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center"}}><div><span style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:900,color:"var(--acc)"}}>₺{t.fiyat}</span><span style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",marginLeft:2}}>/ay</span></div><div style={{background:"var(--blt)",color:"var(--acc)",fontSize:9,fontWeight:700,padding:"4px 10px",borderRadius:6}}>{"Detay →"}</div></div>
  </div>);
}
function TStat({l,v,c}){return(<div style={{textAlign:"center",background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:6,padding:"5px 2px"}}><div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color:c}}>{v}</div><div style={{fontSize:7,color:"var(--txt3)",textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:.3,marginTop:1}}>{l}</div></div>)}
function TariffDetail({t}){
  const hasSart=t.sart&&SART_INFO[t.sart];
  return(<div className="au" style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:16,padding:22,border:"1px solid var(--brd)",boxShadow:"0 4px 20px rgba(37,59,128,.07)",position:"relative",overflow:"hidden"}}>
    <div style={{position:"absolute",top:0,left:0,right:0,height:3,background:"linear-gradient(90deg,var(--acc),var(--tc))"}}/>
    <div style={{position:"relative",zIndex:1}}>
      <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:12,marginBottom:18,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
        <div style={{width:48,height:48,borderRadius:14,background:"var(--blt)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:24}}>{t.ikon}</div>
        <div style={{flex:1,minWidth:120}}><h2 style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--txt)"}}>{t.ad}</h2><div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{t.kategori} • {t.sure} • {t.tip==="faturali"?"Faturalı":"Ön Ödemeli"}</div></div>
        <div style={{textAlign:"right"}}><div style={{fontSize:26,fontWeight:900,color:"var(--acc)"}}>₺{t.fiyat}</div><div style={{fontSize:9,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>/ aylık</div></div>
      </div>
      <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr",gap:10,marginBottom:16}}>
        <BarStat label="🌐 İnternet" value={`${t.gb} GB`} pct={Math.min(t.gb,100)} color="var(--acc)"/><BarStat label="📞 Dakika" value={`${t.dk} dk`} pct={Math.min(t.dk/30,100)} color="#3A5BC7"/><BarStat label="💬 SMS" value={`${t.sms}`} pct={Math.min(t.sms/10,100)} color="#D4548A"/>
      </div>
      <div style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:8,padding:10,marginBottom:14,fontSize:11,color:"var(--txt2)"}}><b style={{color:"var(--txt)"}}>İçerik: </b>{t.icerik}</div>
      {hasSart&&(<div style={{background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:10,padding:12,marginBottom:14,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8}}><span style={{fontSize:22}}>{SART_INFO[t.sart].i}</span><div><div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)"}}>{SART_INFO[t.sart].b} — Şart</div><div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>{SART_INFO[t.sart].a}</div></div></div>)}
      {!hasSart&&t.tip==="faturali"&&<div style={{background:"var(--blt)",borderRadius:8,padding:8,marginBottom:14,textAlign:"center",fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:600}}>Bu tarife için özel şart aranmaz</div>}
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
        <a href={waTariff(t.ad)} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" style={{flex:1,minWidth:140,background:"#25D366",border:"none",borderRadius:10,padding:12,color:"#fff",fontWeight:800,fontSize:13,textDecoration:"none",textAlign:"center",boxShadow:"0 4px 12px rgba(37,166,104,.25)"}}>💬 WhatsApp ile Başvur</a>
        <a href="tel:05326822277" style={{background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:10,padding:"12px 16px",color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:600,fontSize:12,textDecoration:"none"}}>📞 Ara</a>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>);
}
function BarStat({label,value,pct,color}){return(<div style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:10,padding:12}}><div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:4}}><span style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{label}</span><span style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:800,color}}>{value}</span></div><div style={{height:4,background:"var(--brd)",borderRadius:2,overflow:"hidden"}}><div style={{width:`${pct}%`,height:"100%",background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${color},var(--tc))`,borderRadius:2}}/></div></div>)}

/* ═══ AUTH MODAL ═══ */
function AuthModal({onClose,onLogin}){
  const[mode,setMode]=useState("login");const[name,setName]=useState("");const[email,setEmail]=useState("");
  const inp={width:"100%",padding:"10px 12px",background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,color:"var(--txt)",fontSize:12,fontFamily:"inherit",outline:"none"};
  return(<div style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,zIndex:200,background:"rgba(0,0,0,.3)",backdropFilter:"blur(10px)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",padding:16}} onClick={onClose}>
    <div onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()} className="au" style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:16,padding:28,width:360,maxWidth:"100%",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",boxShadow:"0 8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,.12)"}}>
      <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:14}}><img src={LOGO_ICON} alt="Turkcell" style={{height:36,marginBottom:8}}/><h2 style={{fontSize:16,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--acc)"}}>{mode==="login"?"Giriş Yap":"Üye Ol"}</h2><p style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",marginTop:2}}>Elfin İletişim Hesabınız</p></div>
      <button style={{width:"100%",padding:"9px",background:"#fff",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:8,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",gap:6,fontSize:11,fontWeight:600,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",marginBottom:12,color:"var(--txt)"}} onClick={()=>onLogin("Google Kullanıcı")}>
        <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path fill="#4285F4" d="M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92a5.06 5.06 0 01-2.2 3.32v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.1z"/><path fill="#34A853" d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z"/><path fill="#FBBC05" d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z"/><path fill="#EA4335" d="M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z"/></svg>
        Google ile {mode==="login"?"Giriş":"Kayıt"}
      </button>
      <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:6,marginBottom:12}}><div style={{flex:1,height:1,background:"var(--brd)"}}/><span style={{fontSize:8,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>veya</span><div style={{flex:1,height:1,background:"var(--brd)"}}/></div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:7}}>
        {mode==="register"&&<input value={name} onChange={e=>setName(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ad Soyad" style={inp}/>}
        <input value={email} onChange={e=>setEmail(e.target.value)} placeholder="E-posta" style={inp}/>
        <input placeholder="Şifre" type="password" style={inp}/>
        <button onClick={()=>onLogin(name||email.split("@")[0]||"Kullanıcı")} style={{background:"var(--acc)",border:"none",borderRadius:8,padding:10,color:"#fff",fontWeight:800,fontSize:12,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{mode==="login"?"Giriş Yap":"Üye Ol"}</button>
      </div>
      <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginTop:8}}><button onClick={()=>setMode(mode==="login"?"register":"login")} style={{background:"none",border:"none",color:"var(--acc)",fontSize:10,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{mode==="login"?"Hesabınız yok mu? Üye Ol":"Zaten üye misiniz? Giriş Yap"}</button></div>
    </div>
  </div>);
}

/* ═══ ADMIN PANEL ═══ */
function AdminPanel({tariffs,setTariffs,onClose}){
  const[tab,setTab]=useState("info");
  const phoneRef=useRef(null);const tariffRef=useRef(null);
  const[uploadMsg,setUploadMsg]=useState("");
  const[uploadStatus,setUploadStatus]=useState("");// "loading","success","error"
  const[uploadedFiles,setUploadedFiles]=useState([]);

  function handleCSV(file,type){
    if(!file)return;
    setUploadStatus("loading");
    setUploadMsg(`"${file.name}" okunuyor...`);
    const reader=new FileReader();
    reader.onload=(e)=>{
      const text=e.target.result;const lines=text.trim().split("\n");
      if(lines.length<2){setUploadStatus("error");setUploadMsg("❌ Dosya boş veya hatalı. En az 2 satır (başlık + veri) olmalı.");return}
      setUploadStatus("success");
      setUploadMsg(`✅ "${file.name}" başarıyla yüklendi!\n${type}: ${lines.length-1} satır okundu.`);
      setUploadedFiles(prev=>[...prev,{name:file.name,type,rows:lines.length-1,time:new Date().toLocaleTimeString("tr-TR")}]);
    };
    reader.onerror=()=>{setUploadStatus("error");setUploadMsg("❌ Dosya okunamadı. Lütfen tekrar deneyin.")};
    reader.readAsText(file);
  }

  const msgStyle=uploadStatus==="success"
    ?{background:"rgba(13,124,61,.08)",border:"1px solid rgba(13,124,61,.2)",color:"#0d7c3d"}
    :uploadStatus==="error"
    ?{background:"rgba(220,38,38,.08)",border:"1px solid rgba(220,38,38,.2)",color:"#dc2626"}
    :{background:"rgba(37,59,128,.06)",border:"1px solid rgba(37,59,128,.15)",color:"var(--acc)"};

  return(<div style={{position:"fixed",inset:0,zIndex:200,background:"rgba(0,0,0,.3)",backdropFilter:"blur(10px)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",padding:16}} onClick={onClose}>
    <div onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()} className="au" style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:16,padding:28,width:600,maxWidth:"100%",maxHeight:"85vh",overflowY:"auto",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",boxShadow:"0 8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,.12)"}}>
      <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:18}}>
        <h2 style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--acc)"}}>⚙️ Yönetim Paneli</h2>
        <button onClick={onClose} style={{background:"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",color:"var(--txt3)",width:32,height:32,borderRadius:8,fontSize:14,cursor:"pointer"}}>✕</button>
      </div>
      <div style={{display:"flex",gap:6,marginBottom:18}}>
        {[{k:"info",l:"ℹ️ Bilgi"},{k:"phones",l:"📱 Cihazlar"},{k:"tariffs",l:"📡 Tarifeler"}].map(t=>(<button key={t.k} onClick={()=>{setTab(t.k);setUploadMsg("");setUploadStatus("")}} style={{background:tab===t.k?"var(--acc)":"var(--bg2)",color:tab===t.k?"#fff":"var(--txt2)",border:"1px solid "+(tab===t.k?"var(--acc)":"var(--brd)"),borderRadius:8,padding:"7px 14px",fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>{t.l}</button>))}
      </div>

      {tab==="info"&&(<div>
        <div style={{background:"var(--blt)",borderRadius:10,padding:16,marginBottom:14}}>
          <h3 style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:8}}>Mevcut Veriler</h3>
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:8}}>
            {[{l:"Telefon",n:ALL_PHONES.length},{l:"Tablet",n:ALL_TABLET.length},{l:"Notebook",n:ALL_NOTEBOOK.length},{l:"Aksesuar",n:ALL_AKSESUAR.length},{l:"VINN",n:ALL_VINN.length},{l:"Tarife Kategorisi",n:tariffs.length}].map((s,i)=>(
              <div key={i} style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:8,padding:"8px 12px",border:"1px solid var(--brd)"}}><span style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>{s.l}: </span><span style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color:"var(--acc)"}}>{s.n}</span></div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
        {uploadedFiles.length>0&&(<div style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:10,padding:12,marginBottom:14}}>
          <h4 style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--txt)",marginBottom:6}}>📋 Bu Oturumdaki Yüklemeler</h4>
          {uploadedFiles.map((f,i)=>(<div key={i} style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt2)",padding:"3px 0",display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between"}}>
            <span>✅ {f.name} ({f.type}, {f.rows} satır)</span>
            <span style={{color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{f.time}</span>
          </div>))}
        </div>)}
        <div style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--txt2)",lineHeight:1.6}}>
          <p>Bu panel üzerinden CSV dosyaları yükleyerek cihaz ve tarife verilerinizi güncelleyebilirsiniz.</p>
          <p style={{marginTop:8}}>Turkcell'den gelen Excel dosyasını CSV formatına dönüştürüp yükleyin.</p>
          <p style={{marginTop:8,color:"var(--txt3)",fontSize:10}}>Not: Kalıcı güncelleme için verileri bana (Claude'a) gönderin, App.jsx'i güncelleyeyim.</p>
        </div>
      </div>)}

      {tab==="phones"&&(<div>
        <div style={{background:"var(--blt)",borderRadius:10,padding:16,marginBottom:14}}>
          <h3 style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:6}}>📱 Cihaz Verisi Yükle</h3>
          <p style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",marginBottom:10,lineHeight:1.4}}>CSV veya Excel dosyanızı seçin. Sütunlar: marka, model, pesin, taksit3, taksit12, taksit24, taksit36</p>
          <input ref={phoneRef} type="file" accept=".csv,.txt,.tsv,.xlsx" onChange={e=>handleCSV(e.target.files[0],"Cihaz")} style={{display:"none"}}/>
          <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,alignItems:"center"}}>
            <button onClick={()=>phoneRef.current?.click()} style={{background:"var(--acc)",border:"none",borderRadius:8,padding:"10px 20px",color:"#fff",fontWeight:700,fontSize:12,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>📁 Dosya Seç</button>
            {uploadStatus==="loading"&&<span style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)"}}>⏳ Yükleniyor...</span>}
          </div>
        </div>
        {uploadMsg&&<div style={{...msgStyle,borderRadius:8,padding:12,fontSize:11,marginBottom:10,whiteSpace:"pre-line"}}>{uploadMsg}</div>}
        <div style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:8,padding:12}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--txt)",marginBottom:6}}>Mevcut Kayıtlar</div>
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:6}}>
            {[{l:"Telefon",n:ALL_PHONES.length,c:"var(--acc)"},{l:"Tablet",n:ALL_TABLET.length,c:"#3A5BC7"},{l:"Notebook",n:ALL_NOTEBOOK.length,c:"#D4548A"},{l:"Aksesuar",n:ALL_AKSESUAR.length,c:"var(--tcD)"}].map((s,i)=>(
              <div key={i} style={{background:"#fff",borderRadius:6,padding:"6px 10px",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center"}}>
                <span style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt2)"}}>{s.l}</span>
                <span style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:800,color:s.c}}>{s.n}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>)}

      {tab==="tariffs"&&(<div>
        <div style={{background:"var(--blt)",borderRadius:10,padding:16,marginBottom:14}}>
          <h3 style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:6}}>📡 Tarife Verisi Yükle</h3>
          <p style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)",marginBottom:10,lineHeight:1.4}}>CSV dosyanızı seçin. Sütunlar: ad, tip, gb, dakika, sms, fiyat, sure, sart, kategori</p>
          <input ref={tariffRef} type="file" accept=".csv,.txt,.tsv,.xlsx" onChange={e=>handleCSV(e.target.files[0],"Tarife")} style={{display:"none"}}/>
          <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,alignItems:"center"}}>
            <button onClick={()=>tariffRef.current?.click()} style={{background:"var(--acc2)",border:"none",borderRadius:8,padding:"10px 20px",color:"#fff",fontWeight:700,fontSize:12,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit"}}>📁 Dosya Seç</button>
            {uploadStatus==="loading"&&<span style={{fontSize:11,color:"var(--acc)"}}>⏳ Yükleniyor...</span>}
          </div>
        </div>
        {uploadMsg&&<div style={{...msgStyle,borderRadius:8,padding:12,fontSize:11,marginBottom:10,whiteSpace:"pre-line"}}>{uploadMsg}</div>}
        <div style={{background:"var(--bg2)",borderRadius:8,padding:12}}>
          <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:8}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--txt)"}}>Mevcut Tarifeler</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt3)"}}>{tariffs.length} kategori, {tariffs.reduce((a,c)=>a+c.tarifeler.length,0)} tarife</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{maxHeight:250,overflowY:"auto"}}>
            {tariffs.map((c,i)=>(<div key={i} style={{marginBottom:8}}><div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"var(--acc)",marginBottom:2}}>{c.ikon} {c.ad} ({c.tarifeler.length})</div>
              {c.tarifeler.map((t,j)=>(<div key={j} style={{fontSize:10,color:"var(--txt2)",padding:"2px 0",paddingLeft:16}}>• {t.ad} — ₺{t.fiyat}/ay</div>))}
            </div>))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>)}
    </div>
  </div>);
}

/* ═══ CHATBOT (AI + Local + Voice + Widget + Fullpage) ═══ */

function ChatBotSystem({fullPage=false, onClose}){
  const[messages,setMessages]=useState([{role:"assistant",content:"Merhaba! 👋 Ben Elfin İletişim'in dijital asistanıyım. Telefon, tarife, ev interneti, aksesuar... ne sorarsan sor! Sesli de sorabilirsin 🎤"}]);
  const[input,setInput]=useState("");
  const[loading,setLoading]=useState(false);
  const[listening,setListening]=useState(false);
  const[speaking,setSpeaking]=useState(false);
  const chatRef=useRef(null);
  const inputRef=useRef(null);
  const recognitionRef=useRef(null);

  useEffect(()=>{if(chatRef.current)chatRef.current.scrollTop=chatRef.current.scrollHeight},[messages,loading]);
  useEffect(()=>{if(inputRef.current)inputRef.current.focus()},[]);

  const systemPrompt=`${CHATBOT_KB}

EK TALİMATLAR:
- Sen Elfin İletişim'in samimi, sıcak dijital asistanısın. Adın "Elfin Asistan".
- Müşteriye "sen" diye hitap et, abi/abla gibi samimi konuş. Mesela: "Hemen bakayım sana!", "Bu model tam sana göre!", "Bir de şuna bak derim".
- Kısa ve net cevaplar ver (2-4 cümle ideal, uzatma).
- Fiyat sorulduğunda tablodaki NET rakamı ver, yuvarlama.
- Emoji kullan ama abartma (mesaj başına 1-2 yeterli).
- Bilmediğin konuda "Güncel bilgi için bizi ara: 0532 682 22 77 ya da WhatsApp'tan yaz!" de.
- RAKİP KURAL: Vodafone, Türk Telekom veya başka operatörleri ASLA kötüleme, küçümseme veya olumsuz karşılaştırma yapma. Sadece Turkcell'in avantajlarını anlat. Müşteri "Vodafone'dan geliyorum" derse "Süper, hoş geldin! Numara taşıma ile geçiş çok kolay" gibi pozitif karşıla.
- SATIŞA YÖNLENDİR: Her cevabın sonunda nazikçe mağazaya veya WhatsApp'a yönlendir. "Hadi gel mağazada bi bakalım!" veya "WhatsApp'tan yaz, hemen ilgilenelim!" gibi.
- ÖNEMLİ: Tarifeler SADECE yeni hat, MNT ve Switch için geçerlidir. Mevcut faturalı hat tarife değişikliği için "mağazamızı aramanı öneririm" de.
- ÖNEMLİ: Yapboz tarifesi ARTIK YOKTUR, bunu sorarlarsa "Maalesef Yapboz kalktı ama sana daha uygun seçeneklerimiz var!" de.
- Switch = Kontörlü Turkcell'den faturalı Turkcell'e geçiş. Başka operatörden değil.
- WhatsApp: 0532 682 22 77
- Telefon: 0532 682 22 77
- Çalışma saatleri: Hafta içi ve Cumartesi 09:00-22:00, Pazar 11:00-22:00
- Cevaplarını düz metin yaz, markdown formatı (**, ##, vb.) KULLANMA.
- Konu dışı sorularda (politika, din, kişisel sorular vb.) "Ben sadece Elfin İletişim ürün ve hizmetleri konusunda yardımcı olabilirim 😊" de.`;

  /* ── SPEECH RECOGNITION ── */
  const startListening=()=>{
    const SR=window.SpeechRecognition||window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
    if(!SR){alert("Tarayıcınız ses tanımayı desteklemiyor.");return}
    const r=new SR();r.lang="tr-TR";r.continuous=false;r.interimResults=true;
    recognitionRef.current=r;
    r.onstart=()=>setListening(true);
    r.onresult=(e)=>{let t="";for(let i=0;i<e.results.length;i++){t+=e.results[i][0].transcript}setInput(t)};
    r.onerror=()=>setListening(false);
    r.onend=()=>{setListening(false);setTimeout(()=>{const el=document.getElementById("elfin-send");if(el)el.click()},400)};
    r.start();
  };
  const stopListening=()=>{if(recognitionRef.current){recognitionRef.current.stop();setListening(false)}};

  /* ── SPEECH SYNTHESIS ── */
  const speakText=(text)=>{
    if(!window.speechSynthesis)return;
    window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
    const clean=text.replace(/[📱📡💰⚡🎁📍🎓🌿👶🏛️🧩📦📞💬📸🌐🏢📋🗺️🤖👋😊✅ℹ️👑🎯💳🔍🎧💻🚋🚶•→←⚠️🔊🎤]/g,"").replace(/\n+/g,". ").replace(/₺/g," TL ").trim();
    const u=new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(clean);u.lang="tr-TR";u.rate=1.05;
    const voices=window.speechSynthesis.getVoices();
    const tv=voices.find(v=>v.lang.startsWith("tr"));if(tv)u.voice=tv;
    u.onstart=()=>setSpeaking(true);u.onend=()=>setSpeaking(false);u.onerror=()=>setSpeaking(false);
    window.speechSynthesis.speak(u);
  };
  const stopSpeaking=()=>{window.speechSynthesis.cancel();setSpeaking(false)};

  /* ── LOCAL FALLBACK ── */
  const localReply=(q)=>{
    const low=q.toLowerCase().replace(/[?!.,]/g,"").trim();
    const has=(...kw)=>kw.some(k=>low.includes(k));

    if(has("merhaba","selam","hey","naber","iyi günler")) return "Merhaba! 😊 Hoş geldiniz Elfin İletişim'e. Size nasıl yardımcı olabilirim?";
    if(has("teşekkür","sağol","eyvallah")) return "Rica ederim! 😊 Başka sorunuz olursa buradayım. WhatsApp: 0532 682 22 77 💬";
    if(has("adres","nerede","konum")) return "📍 Konya Zafer Meydanı'ndayız!\nİhsaniye Mah. Beyhekim Sok. No:2/1 Selçuklu/KONYA\nAlaaddin Tepesi yanı, Tramvay durağı karşısı";
    if(has("telefon num","iletişim","whatsapp","wp","ara")) return "📞 Telefon: 0532 682 22 77\n💬 WhatsApp: 0532 682 22 77\n📸 Instagram: @elfiniletisim\n🕐 Hİ+Cmt 09:00-22:00, Pzr 11:00-22:00";
    if(has("saat","kaçta","açık mı","kapalı")) return "🕐 Çalışma saatlerimiz:\nHafta içi + Cumartesi: 09:00-22:00\nPazar: 11:00-22:00";
    if(has("kampanya","fırsat","çekiliş","hediye","200 tl")) return "🎁 200 TL alışveriş çeki — Faturalıya geçiş/yeni hat alımına!\niPhone 15 çekilişi — 2026 sonuna kadar!\nDetay: 0532 682 22 77 💬";
    if(has("5g")) return "⚡ 1 Nisan 2026'da 5G başlıyor!\n5G modeller: Galaxy S25, Vivo Y29S, iPhone 15, Samsung A17 5G\nSuperbox 5G paketleri de mevcut!";
    if(has("yapboz")) return "Maalesef Yapboz tarifesi sona erdi. Ama size uygun başka harika tarifelerimiz var! Ne tür bir tarife arıyorsunuz? 😊";
    if(has("switch")) return "Switch = Kontörlü (faturasız) Turkcell hattınızı faturalıya geçirmek. Aynı numara kalır. Prestij ve Bol Star gibi avantajlı tarife seçenekleri var. Detay için mağazamızı arayın: 0532 682 22 77";
    if(has("hat bedel","hat ücret","hat fiyat","yeni hat")) return "💳 Yeni hat açılış bedeli: 1.250 TL\nFaturalıda 12 taksit (~104 TL/ay)\nÖn ödemelide peşin ödenir.";
    if(has("sim değ","sim kart")) return "SIM değişikliği: 180 TL";
    if(has("devir","hat devir")) return "Hat devir ücreti: 79 TL";
    if(has("taahhüt","cayma")) return "Taahhüt kapama: Faturalı 875 TL, Kontratlı 350 TL";

    if(has("fiber","ev internet","internet")) return "🏠 Ev interneti seçeneklerimiz:\nFiber: 100-1000 Mbps (800-1.000 TL/ay)\nUltra Fiber: 2-10 Giga\nTaahhütsüz: 750 TL'den başlayan\nSuperbox: Kablosuz ev interneti\nDetay için: 0532 682 22 77";
    if(has("superbox")) return "📡 Superbox: Kablosuz ev interneti!\n300 GB: 1.000 TL/ay\n1 TB: 1.700 TL/ay\n5G Superbox da mevcut!\nFiber olmayan yerlerde ideal.";
    if(has("tv+","netflix","tv plus")) return "📺 TV+ paketleri: 295 TL'den başlayan fiyatlarla!\nFiber + TV+ kombine paketler de var.\nNetflix dahil paketler mevcut.";

    if(has("emekli")){return "🌿 Mutlu Emekli (65 yaş+, faturalı):\n5 GB: 300 TL/ay\n10 GB: 350 TL/ay\n20 GB: 440 TL/ay\n30 GB: 550 TL/ay\nÖn ödemeli: Emektar paketleri de mevcut!"}
    if(has("genç","öğrenci")){return "🎓 Genç Avantaj+ (7-26 yaş, faturalı):\n5 GB: 300 TL/ay\n10 GB: 350 TL/ay\n20 GB: 400 TL/ay\n40 GB: 650 TL/ay\nSinema bileti hediye! Ön ödemeli genç paketleri de var."}
    if(has("çocuk","ilk turkcell","favorim")){return "👶 İlk Turkcellim (7-15 yaş):\n6 GB: 240 TL/ay\n12 GB: 280 TL/ay\n18 GB: 380 TL/ay\nMutlu Çocuk paketleri de mevcut!"}
    if(has("emek","öğretmen","sağlık","çiftçi","kamu")){return "🏛️ Emek (Çiftçi/Öğretmen/Sağlık):\n5 GB: 280 TL/ay\n10 GB: 320 TL/ay\n20 GB: 400 TL/ay\n30 GB: 500 TL/ay\nBelge gerekli."}
    if(has("esnaf","avantaj+")) return "Esnaf Avantaj+ paketleri:\n5 GB: 350 TL/ay\n10 GB: 400 TL/ay\n20 GB: 500 TL/ay\n30 GB: 600 TL/ay\n50 GB Platinum: 800 TL/ay";
    if(has("prestij")) return "Prestij paketleri (Switch için):\n5 GB: 400 TL/ay\n10 GB: 500 TL/ay\n20 GB: 600 TL/ay\n40 GB: 800 TL/ay\nBol Star Fırsat ve Prestij Fırsat da mevcut!";
    if(has("kontörlü","ön ödemeli","faturasız","prepaid")){return "📦 Ön ödemeli hat alınca:\n50 GB + 1000 DK + 250 SMS hoşgeldin paketi (2 ay)\nSonra 3 ay indirimli Cepte Yeni paketler.\nCepte Yeni 10 GB: 175 TL, 20 GB: 225 TL"}
    if(has("rahat")) return "Rahat Ol paketleri:\n2 GB: 290 TL\n4 GB: 310 TL\n9 GB: 370 TL\n14 GB: 430 TL\n18 GB: 470 TL";
    if(has("data","sadece internet")) return "Data paketleri (sadece internet):\n10 GB: 315 TL\n20 GB: 415 TL\n50 GB: 535 TL\n100 GB: 635 TL";
    if(has("turist","tourist")) return "Turist paketleri:\n20 GB: 250 TL (28 gün)\n50 GB: 530 TL (28 gün)";
    if(has("asker","askercell")) return "Askercell İkili: 20 TL — 1000 DK + 1000 SMS";
    if(has("saat","akıllı saat")) return "Akıllı çocuk saati paketleri:\n1 GB: 80 TL\n2 GB: 90 TL\n5 GB: 110 TL";
    if(has("mobil wifi")) return "Mobil WiFi (faturasız data):\n25 GB: 430 TL\n50 GB: 550 TL\n100 GB: 650 TL\n200 GB: 830 TL";
    if(has("mnt","numara taşıma","operatör","vodafone","türk telekom")) return "📱 Numara taşıma (MNT):\nVodafone/Türk Telekom'dan Turkcell'e geçin!\nNumaranız korunur, 1-3 iş günü.\nTaahhüt: 1 yıl\nGerekli: Kimlik + eski operatör fatura";

    if(has("tarife")) {
      return "📡 Tarife kategorilerimiz:\n\nFaturalı: Prestij, Genç, Emekli, Emek, Esnaf, Rahat, Çocuk, Data\nÖn Ödemeli: Cepte Yeni, Başlangıç, Hemen, Genç, Emektar\nEv İnterneti: Fiber, Superbox, TV+\n\nHangi kategoriyi merak ediyorsunuz?";
    }

    if(has("iphone")){return "📱 iPhone modelleri:\niPhone 13 128GB: 38.959 TL\niPhone 14 128GB: 43.539 TL\niPhone 15 128GB: 48.999 TL\niPhone 16E 128GB: 43.999 TL\niPhone 17 256GB: 68.499 TL\niPhone 17 Pro 256GB: 107.989 TL\niPhone Air 256GB: 89.999 TL\n3-36 ay taksit mevcut!"}
    if(has("samsung")){return "📱 Samsung modelleri:\nGalaxy A07: 8.979 TL\nGalaxy A17: 12.989 TL\nGalaxy A26 5G: 15.399 TL\nGalaxy S25 256GB: 64.799 TL\nDaha fazla model için mağazamızı arayın!"}
    if(has("xiaomi","redmi")){return "📱 Xiaomi modelleri:\nRedmi 15C: 8.999 TL\nRedmi Note 15: 20.989 TL\nRedmi 15T: 33.999 TL"}
    if(has("telefon","cihaz")){return "📱 227 telefon modelimiz var! Apple, Samsung, Xiaomi ve daha fazlası.\nBütçenizi söyleyin, size uygun önereyim! 😊"}
    if(has("en ucuz","uygun fiyat","ucuz")){return "💰 Uygun fiyatlı telefonlar:\nSamsung Galaxy A07: 8.979 TL\nXiaomi Redmi 15C: 8.999 TL\nSamsung Galaxy A17: 12.989 TL"}
    if(has("taksit")){return "💳 Cihaz taksit: 3, 6, 12, 24, 36 ay seçenekleri mevcut. Model ve taksit detayı için mağazamızı arayın: 0532 682 22 77"}

    return null;
  };

  /* ── AI REPLY ── */
  const aiReply=async(allMsgs)=>{
    const apiMsgs=allMsgs.filter(m=>m.role!=="system").map(m=>({role:m.role,content:m.content})).slice(-12);
    const res=await fetch("/api/chat",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},body:JSON.stringify({messages:apiMsgs,system:systemPrompt})});
    if(!res.ok)throw new Error("API error");
    const data=await res.json();if(data.error)throw new Error(data.error);
    return data.reply;
  };

  /* ── SEND ── */
  const handleSend=async(text)=>{
    const msg=text||input.trim();
    if(!msg||loading)return;
    const updated=[...messages,{role:"user",content:msg}];
    setMessages(updated);setInput("");setLoading(true);

    let reply;
    try{reply=await aiReply(updated)}
    catch(e){reply=localReply(msg)||"Şu an AI asistana ulaşamıyorum ama yardımcı olayım! 😊\n\nSorabilirsiniz:\n📱 Telefon fiyatları\n📡 Tarife bilgisi\n🏠 Ev interneti\n📍 Mağaza bilgisi\n\nWhatsApp: 0532 682 22 77 💬"}

    setMessages(prev=>[...prev,{role:"assistant",content:reply}]);
    setLoading(false);
    if(reply.length<250)setTimeout(()=>speakText(reply),500);
  };

  const containerStyle=fullPage?{width:"100%",height:"calc(100vh - 60px)",background:"#fff",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column"}:{width:370,maxWidth:"calc(100vw - 32px)",height:540,maxHeight:"calc(100vh - 100px)",background:"#fff",borderRadius:20,boxShadow:"0 8px 40px rgba(37,59,128,.2)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",overflow:"hidden"};

  return(
    <div className={fullPage?"":"chat-panel"} style={containerStyle}>
      {/* Header */}
      <div style={{background:"var(--acc)",padding:fullPage?"16px 20px":"12px 16px",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"space-between",flexShrink:0}}>
        <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:10}}>
          <div style={{width:38,height:38,borderRadius:19,background:"var(--tc)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:20}}>🤖</div>
          <div>
            <div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,color:"#fff"}}>Elfin Asistan</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:"rgba(255,255,255,.7)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:4}}>
              <span style={{width:6,height:6,borderRadius:3,background:"#25D366",display:"inline-block"}}></span>
              {listening?"🎤 Dinliyor...":speaking?"🔊 Konuşuyor...":"Çevrimiçi"}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:6}}>
          {speaking&&<button onClick={stopSpeaking} style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.2)",border:"none",color:"#fff",width:32,height:32,borderRadius:16,fontSize:14,cursor:"pointer",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}>🔇</button>}
          {onClose&&<button onClick={()=>{stopSpeaking();stopListening();onClose()}} style={{background:"rgba(255,255,255,.15)",border:"none",color:"#fff",width:32,height:32,borderRadius:16,fontSize:16,cursor:"pointer",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}>✕</button>}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Messages */}
      <div ref={chatRef} style={{flex:1,overflowY:"auto",padding:"12px",display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:8,background:"var(--bg2)",WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
        {messages.map((m,i)=>(
          <div key={i} style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:m.role==="user"?"flex-end":"flex-start",alignItems:"flex-end",gap:6}}>
            {m.role==="assistant"&&<div style={{width:26,height:26,borderRadius:13,background:"var(--tc)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:13,flexShrink:0}}>🤖</div>}
            <div style={{maxWidth:"80%",position:"relative"}}>
              <div style={{padding:"10px 14px",borderRadius:m.role==="user"?"16px 16px 4px 16px":"16px 16px 16px 4px",background:m.role==="user"?"var(--acc)":"#fff",color:m.role==="user"?"#fff":"var(--txt)",fontSize:13,lineHeight:1.55,boxShadow:m.role==="user"?"none":"0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06)",wordBreak:"break-word",whiteSpace:"pre-line"}}>{m.content}</div>
              {m.role==="assistant"&&i>0&&<button onClick={()=>speakText(m.content)} style={{position:"absolute",bottom:-2,right:-2,width:22,height:22,borderRadius:11,background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",color:"var(--acc)",fontSize:10,cursor:"pointer",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}>🔊</button>}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading&&(
          <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"flex-end",gap:6}}>
            <div style={{width:26,height:26,borderRadius:13,background:"var(--tc)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:13}}>🤖</div>
            <div style={{background:"#fff",padding:"12px 18px",borderRadius:"16px 16px 16px 4px",boxShadow:"0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06)",display:"flex",gap:4}}>
              {[0,1,2].map(i=>(<div key={i} style={{width:7,height:7,borderRadius:"50%",background:"var(--txt3)",animation:`chatDot 1.4s ${i*.2}s infinite ease-in-out both`}} />))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Quick Actions */}
      <div style={{padding:"5px 12px",display:"flex",gap:4,overflowX:"auto",flexShrink:0,background:"#fff",borderTop:"1px solid var(--brd)",WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
        {["📱 Telefon fiyat","📡 Tarife öner","🏠 Ev interneti","⚡ 5G modeller","🎁 Kampanyalar","📍 Adres","💬 Switch nedir"].map((q,i)=>(<button key={i} onClick={()=>handleSend(q)} style={{flex:"0 0 auto",background:"var(--blt)",border:"1px solid var(--brd)",borderRadius:16,padding:"4px 11px",fontSize:10,color:"var(--acc)",fontWeight:600,cursor:"pointer",fontFamily:"inherit",whiteSpace:"nowrap"}}>{q}</button>))}
      </div>

      {/* Input + Mic */}
      <div style={{padding:"8px 12px 10px",display:"flex",gap:6,alignItems:"center",background:"#fff",borderTop:"1px solid var(--brd)",flexShrink:0}}>
        <button onClick={listening?stopListening:startListening} style={{width:40,height:40,borderRadius:20,background:listening?"#FF4444":"var(--blt)",border:listening?"none":"1px solid var(--brd)",color:listening?"#fff":"var(--acc)",fontSize:16,cursor:"pointer",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",flexShrink:0,animation:listening?"pulse5g 1s infinite":"none"}}>🎤</button>
        <input ref={inputRef} value={input} onChange={e=>setInput(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e=>{if(e.key==="Enter"&&!e.shiftKey)handleSend()}}
          placeholder={listening?"Dinliyorum...":"Mesajınızı yazın veya 🎤 basın"}
          style={{flex:1,padding:"10px 14px",background:listening?"rgba(255,68,68,.06)":"var(--bg2)",border:"1px solid "+(listening?"#FF4444":"var(--brd)"),borderRadius:20,color:"var(--txt)",fontSize:13,fontFamily:"inherit",outline:"none"}} />
        <button id="elfin-send" onClick={()=>handleSend()} disabled={!input.trim()||loading}
          style={{width:40,height:40,borderRadius:20,background:input.trim()&&!loading?"var(--acc)":"var(--bg2)",border:"none",color:input.trim()&&!loading?"#fff":"var(--txt3)",fontSize:16,cursor:input.trim()&&!loading?"pointer":"default",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",flexShrink:0}}>➤</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ── Widget (Floating) ── */
function ChatBot(){
  const[open,setOpen]=useState(false);
  return(<>
    {!open&&<div style={{position:"fixed",bottom:20,right:20,zIndex:95}}>
      <div style={{position:"absolute",top:-8,right:-4,background:"var(--acc)",color:"#fff",fontSize:7,fontWeight:800,padding:"2px 6px",borderRadius:8,whiteSpace:"nowrap",boxShadow:"0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.2)"}}>AI Destekli</div>
      <button onClick={()=>setOpen(true)} style={{width:56,height:56,borderRadius:28,background:"linear-gradient(135deg,var(--tc),#ff9500)",color:"#000",border:"none",fontSize:24,cursor:"pointer",boxShadow:"0 4px 20px rgba(255,199,44,.4)",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",transition:"all .2s"}} onMouseEnter={e=>e.currentTarget.style.transform="scale(1.1)"} onMouseLeave={e=>e.currentTarget.style.transform="scale(1)"}>💬</button>
    </div>}
    {open&&<div style={{position:"fixed",bottom:16,right:16,zIndex:200}}><ChatBotSystem onClose={()=>setOpen(false)} /></div>}
  </>);
}

/* ── Full Page Chat ── */
function ChatFullPage(){
  return(
    <div className="au" style={{paddingTop:0}}>
      <ChatBotSystem fullPage={true} />
    </div>
  );
}

function Empty(){return <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"36px 16px",color:"var(--txt3)"}}><div style={{fontSize:32,opacity:.3,marginBottom:8}}>🔍</div><p style={{fontSize:12}}>Kriterlere uygun sonuç bulunamadı.</p></div>}
